Legislative Yuan Passes

Full Text of the Amnesty Law

The Legislative Yuan held its 188th meeting at 8:00 AM on the 11th and passed the Amnesty Law. The full text is as follows: (Article 1) All crimes committed before March 5, 1931, for which the heaviest principal punishment is imprisonment for two years or less, detention, or a specific fine, are hereby pardoned. The same applies to crimes punishable solely by deprivation of public rights or confiscation. (Article 2) Except for those pardoned under the preceding article, for other crimes with the heaviest principal punishment being death, life imprisonment, or imprisonment for seven years or more, the sentence shall be reduced by

one-third. For those with a sentence of less than seven years, the sentence shall be reduced by one-half. However, the following types of crimes are not eligible for sentence reduction: (1) Crimes of treason; (2) Murder of a direct ascendant relative; (3) Murder that is premeditated or involves cruel acts; (4) Robbery or piracy resulting in intentional homicide; (5) Robbery or piracy involving arson or rape; (6) Kidnapping for ransom resulting in intentional homicide or rape of the victim; (7) Rape resulting in intentional homicide of the victim; (8) Transferring a person enticed or abducted outside the territory of the Republic of China; (9) Crimes of dereliction of duty or embezzlement of public funds; (10) Crimes defined by special criminal laws that are of the same nature as the above clauses. (Article 3) Those who have committed crimes under the Emergency Punishment Law for Endangering the Republic of China or the old Provisional Anti-Revolutionary Punishment Law and have been pardoned shall be transferred to a rehabilitation center if they are deemed to still pose a threat to the Republic of China. (Article 4) Pardoned criminals other than those mentioned in the preceding article shall be subject to the Re-offending Prevention Law for prevention if they are deemed likely to re-offend. The Re-offending Prevention Law shall be determined by the Ministry of Judicial Administration. (Article 5) For pardoned criminals who have already been sentenced and whose sentences have become final, the chief prosecutor of the High Court shall approve their release and report to the Ministry of Judicial Administration. For criminals sentenced by military tribunals, the competent military authorities shall approve their release and report separately to the Ministry of Military Affairs or the Ministry of the Navy. For those who have not been sentenced, in addition to handling the matter in accordance with the provisions of the Criminal Procedure Law regarding amnesty, the names, genders, places of origin, and details of the cases of the criminals shall be reported. (Article 6) Those who have already been sentenced to life imprisonment shall have their sentences reduced to imprisonment for a fixed term, and those who have been sentenced to imprisonment for a fixed term at the highest degree shall have the number of days already served counted towards the reduced term. Those who have been explicitly granted sentence reduction shall be granted a further reduction based on the reduced sentence. (Article 7) Sentence reduction in cases where sentences have already become final shall be carried out by the court of last instance that reviewed the facts or by other equivalent authorities by means of a ruling. For those who have not been sentenced, the sentence reduction shall be carried out at the time of the judgment. (Article 8) This law shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Military-Police Joint Inspection Measures: Recently, robberies have frequently occurred in the areas near Songjiang, posing a threat to local security. Various local agencies, due to the recent end of the Shanghai War, are concerned that scattered soldiers may be hiding and causing trouble, and have recognized the need to organize joint military-police inspections to curb banditry. Yesterday, the county government invited the provincial security forces, the 88th Division, the tax police corps, and their respective officers to a meeting to discuss measures to maintain public order. It was decided that it was necessary to organize joint military-police inspections. Therefore, it was decided that the four military-police agencies would each contribute fourteen personnel to be stationed at the Yue Temple and the county government. Starting from Monday, they will patrol in groups, and the security corps will dispatch soldiers to guard the four city gates to check for criminals. Local public order should be stabilized.

Qingpu

County Education Association Strives for Education Funds: The County Education Association previously noted that the County Education Bureau intended to reduce the allocation of education funds for one month due to the shortfall in the collection of the grain tax surcharge last year. The association argued that the lives of school staff were already very difficult, and they had been indirectly affected by the Shanghai War, and it was more appropriate to find ways to provide relief rather than reduce education funds. Therefore, the association's eleventh executive committee meeting resolved to send a letter to the County Education Bureau to strongly argue for maintaining the original education funds, and to submit a petition to the county magistrate to order the Finance Bureau to strictly continue to collect the outstanding grain tax to enrich the local economy and benefit the development of education. It is learned that in addition to earnestly implementing the above resolution, Zhao Yunzang, the standing director of the association, also explained to Chen, the department head of the county government, and Yuan, the director of the Education Bureau, the hardship of not being able to reduce education funds, and requested them to find ways to support it. It is heard that Chen, the department head of the county government, highly values education as it relates to the local community, and is doing his best to assist. He has also contacted Director Yuan once, and the bureau is no longer able to insist on the proposed reduction of funds. Therefore, the proposal to reduce education funds is unlikely to become a reality.

Suzhou

Notorious Bandit Li Zhixiang Apprehended: Li Zhixiang, also known as Li Heipi, the ringleader of a gang that robbed the Damao area of Wujiang County and kidnapped twenty-three people, was wanted by the Third District of the Water Police. Subsequently, Director Shen sent detectives to the Shanghai Concession, where the bandit was captured and handed over to the local branch court. Yesterday (the 10th), detectives escorted the bandit to Suzhou and sent him to the district headquarters for interrogation.

Wuxi

Rice-Snatching Trend Spreads Throughout the County: This county suffered a disaster last year, and this year it has been affected by the Shanghai war. The silkworm market is also hopeless, leading to a desperate social and economic situation. The strong resort to taking risks, while the weak are left to perish. Therefore, the trend of snatching rice and robbing has occurred from time to time. Initially, rice-snatching was most prevalent in the seventh district, but it has since spread to the eighth and tenth districts. Now, it seems to be spreading throughout the entire county. On the night of the 7th of this month, at the home of Zhou Fen in Yangjiawan, District 10, fifteen or sixteen poor people wearing black headscarves suddenly broke down the door. They tied up Zhou, her son Renbao, and her daughter-in-law Chen, and beat them severely. They snatched four piculs of white rice, a gold ring, and three boxes of clothes. Renbao then took a gong to the roof and made a commotion, but he was dragged down by the bandits and struck in the jaw, rendering him immobile. Zhou's grandson Zuxing and granddaughter Rongzhen were also terrified. Afterwards, Zhou did not report the incident to the county to request an arrest. Unexpectedly, on the night of the 9th, another fifteen or sixteen similar poor people came, broke down the door, tied up the family members, and beat them severely. They again snatched four piculs of white rice, five cotton quilts, and a box of old clothes before fleeing. The total loss from both incidents is estimated at three or four hundred yuan.

Security Chief Captures Two Communists: Zhu Meiji, the security chief of the eighth district of this county, previously captured two communists, Pu Gengsheng and Tao Axiao, who had shot and killed Pu Tongqing, in Punanwang, District Nine, and Anzhen, District Eight. They also recovered a Mauser pistol and two handguns. They admitted to shooting and killing Jiang Agen and their accomplice Cai Yonggeng, as well as robbing Chen Guilin's family of rice. Yesterday (the 11th) at 11:00 AM, Zhu, along with his team, escorted them to the city, presented them to the county government, and after interrogation by the department head, ordered them to be detained for investigation.

Jiangyin

Investigation of Cai Zhongwei Case Completed and Reported: The Military Affairs Commission consulted the provincial government to order Magistrate Ma to investigate and report on the case of Cai Zhongwei, the captain of the Fourth Team of the Engineering Training Office of the Military and Political Department, who was accused of intimidating farmers and privately receiving subsidies in Houcheng in April. This case was previously reported in the newspaper. Now, Min Junzhong, the director of the Third Public Security Branch, sent inspector Chen Liang to the Second District Office to investigate. According to Shen Dander, the district chief, Cai Zhongwei led his team to the area in early April and requested food and reward money. The first time, ten silver dollars were given, the second time twenty dollars, and the third time seventy dollars. Several days later, Cai again requested rewards, and Cheng Yinfu, the assistant of this district, managed to give him eighty silver dollars. Several times in total, a total of one hundred and eighty silver dollars was rewarded, and there was no receipt. It is confirmed that when supervising the digging of trenches, Dai Xingren, the acting chief of Lei Dong Township, slapped Cai three times and unreasonably intimidated the farmers, saying that anyone who disobeyed orders would be shot. Director Min will report the findings to the county government through the general bureau and forward them to the provincial government for reply to the Military Affairs Commission for investigation.

They requested that Wu be removed from office immediately.

Gaoyou

Two Women Commit Suicide After Leaking Love Affairs: Chen, the wife of Wang, a blacksmith in Lingtangqiao, Huxi, a county district, learned that Jin, the wife of Zhang Dafa, had an affair with someone. She widely publicized this, and Jin questioned Chen, as her reputation was at stake. The two sides had a conflict of words and scolded each other. Zhang Dafa learned of this and severely reprimanded his wife. Jin, feeling ashamed and in debt, had thoughts of ending her life. That night, she secretly swallowed several opium bubbles. By the time people discovered it, she had already died. Chen felt remorseful and also committed suicide by taking opium paste. It was truly tragic.

Yangzhou

The Grand Canal Project Stalled Due to Lack of Funds: The Grand Canal project, due to the suspension of funds, cannot be completed as scheduled. The critical situation has been reported in this newspaper. Now, people from Jiangbei have been sending telegrams requesting assistance. The telegrams are listed below: (1) The Jiangbei Flood Relief Association, Hu Zhen, Wang Jingting, Bao Xiangzhong, etc., telegraphed Ye Chucang to urgently expedite funding in Beijing, stating that the disaster in Jiangbei was caused by the breach of the dikes and that the construction was about to be completed. The telegram stated, "The heavenly disaster in Jiangbei has been tragically caused by the breach of the dikes. As the great project is about to be completed, we were celebrating together. Suddenly, we heard that there was a lack of funds, and there are signs that work will be suspended. All the work will be lost, and the disaster will be irreversible. The disaster is imminent, and we cannot remain silent. The national government has pledged one million yuan in aid, but the Ministry of Railways has only allocated one-tenth of that amount. You have consistently provided relief, and your contributions are for the people. We urge you to quickly present the situation to the national government and transfer all the promised funds to Yangzhou as soon as possible. This is the only way to reverse the disaster and prevent all previous efforts from being wasted. The survival of the canal dikes depends on this one action. We urgently await your instructions." (2) Jiangbei citizens Xia Zhongjin, Yan Weihan, Yin Xiaoqi, and others telegraphed the Rehabilitation Committee, stating, "Repairing the canal dikes will take place in five months, and the quality of the project is visible. We dare not blindly criticize, but with the flood approaching, the work is not yet complete, and two-thirds of it remains. Pausing the work will make it impossible to finish, The rehabilitation fund is in a lack of funds, and they cannot fully assist them. The office in Yangzhou cannot cope with the demands, causing panic at the moment. The mountain is only a basketful away from being finished, the committee must push for the completion. The committee will not make progress due to a lack of a basket full, and the aim of saving people from start to finish will be unfulfilled.

The committee will have the strength to be well prepared, in order to prevent stopping the engineering. Please specify clearly, to settle people’s hearts." (3) Zhu Shiseng telegraphed Wang Yiting in Shanghai, stating, "The Jiangbei river project urgently needs funds. Work has been suspended due to the lack of funds. The customs surcharge of 800,000 yuan has been approved by the national government and designated for the Jiangbei river project. I am now seeking to discuss this with Mr. Zhu Ziqiao to quickly allocate these funds to provide relief and alleviate the current emergency.

If this is not enough, 400,000 yuan can ensure a satisfactory outcome. Mr. Zi is very anxious about this and urges you to consider the suffering of the people in Jiangbei and proceed quickly. I am eagerly awaiting your reply." It is also heard that Vice Chairman Han of the office in Yangzhou hastily crossed the river yesterday to discuss the matter with Chairman Gu and the heads of the Department of Finance and Construction.

Pinghu

Petition to Ban Fast Boats: The Pinghu-Shanghai and Pinghu-Minnan shipping companies, which operate between Pinghu and Shanghai, have been adding more ships and increasing their speed due to business competition in recent years. This has caused severe erosion of farmland in the Xindai area. The first meeting of the county representatives previously resolved to ban the operation of fast boats, but this has been ignored. Now, the village committees along the line have submitted dozens of photographs showing the erosion of farmland and the overloaded weight of the boats, requesting the Department of Construction to strictly prohibit the operation of fast boats in order to protect farmland.

According to reliable sources, Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Central Military Commission, intends to establish a defense command in Ningbo to consolidate the defense of eastern Zhejiang and facilitate the command of various armies. The command will be responsible for all combat readiness and alert matters within the defense area, which includes the Zhenhai Fortress area, the sea police district of the Water Police Bureau, and the surrounding areas of Ningbo. Chairman Chiang has already ordered the Ministry of Military Administration to appoint Wang Haonan as the commander. It is also reported that the command headquarters will be established within the month, and the Zhenhai Fortress Command has received instructions from the military headquarters.

The Ministry of Education Orders the Suspension of Labor University

Teachers and Students Jointly Protect the School

The Executive Yuan of the National Government resolved to suspend the Labor University at its 39th meeting on June 7th, but this was not announced in the newspapers until the Ministry of Education ordered the school on the 11th to completely close down at the end of this academic year and transfer students from all classes in the next term to other national universities. Upon receiving the order, the teachers and students of the school were deeply indignant and immediately convened a full meeting of faculty and staff at Labor Father Road at 2:00 PM on the 11th. Zhang Yuanzhu was elected as the chairman, and Kang Xuanyi as the recorder. It was immediately decided to form a school protection committee, and Xun Fanzhengbo, Tang Ying, Han Yanmen, Kang Xuanyi, Li Yingbiao, Lin Tongshi, Zhang Yuanruo, Ju Shouzheng, Chen Zhenyu, Wang Chengyin, Shen Mingpan, Ding Yao, Lin Zuxin, Xu Yanzhi, Liao Songyun, and 15 others were elected as executive committee members to be responsible for the progress. A written statement refuting the order of the Ministry of Education will be drafted tonight, and representatives will be sent to visit the founders of the school, Li Shizeng, Cai Yuanpei, Chu Minyi, and Wu Zhihui, to request their assistance in this endeavor.

All the students of the school also held a general meeting in the temporary school building at 10:00 AM yesterday, during which they organized a student school protection committee and pledged to work hard to protect the school and not stop until the goal of enrollment is achieved. It is reported that the students are extremely indignant that the Ministry of Education did not consider the restoration of the school after the losses in the Shanghai war but instead ordered its suspension. If necessary, all the students will go to the capital to petition.

Municipal Bureau of Education

Restrictions on Summer Schools This Year

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued instructions to all levels of schools in the city to restrict the operation of summer schools this year, stating that due to the impact of the war, most schools in the city started later, and the teaching dates should be extended during the summer vacation to make up for classes. Therefore, there must be considerable restrictions on schools operating summer schools. Only schools that started earlier and have already completed the formal curriculum for this semester may hold them and should comply with the "Rules for Supervising Summer Schools" promulgated by this Bureau and apply to this Bureau for approval in advance. In addition to distribution, the original rules are copied and issued for all levels of schools in this city to comply with. Attached is a copy of the Rules for Supervising Summer Schools of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education.

Rules for Supervising Summer Schools of the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education

1. The regulations of these rules shall be uniformly applied to all summer schools established in this city and shall be supervised by this Bureau. 2. The students admitted to summer schools shall comply with the Ministry's order and be limited to students and faculty of secondary schools or above or other civil servants. 3. The academic performance of students in summer schools shall not be considered as formal credits or length of study, according to the Ministry's order. 4. The tuition fee for summer schools shall be limited to one silver dollar per week for each hour of university instruction and five jiao for secondary schools. If the instruction is more than one hour, it shall be calculated accordingly. 5. Elementary schools may set up summer remedial classes, and the fee for each student per term shall be limited to one dollar. 6. To establish a summer school, the founder shall fill out a form with the following items and submit it to the Bureau for approval: 1. Name, 2. Location, 3. Purpose (whether for teachers or civil servants to take advanced courses or for students to receive remedial instruction), 4. Name, resume, and address of the founder, 5. A list of the principal and faculty, 6. A list of the curriculum. A copy of the constitution shall be attached when applying. 7. The Bureau shall send personnel to inspect summer schools at any time, and if any violation of these rules or other inappropriate circumstances occur, the Bureau may take corrective action. 8. Summer schools shall submit the names of students and the grades of each subject to this Bureau for verification at the end of the term. 9. These rules shall be implemented after being submitted to the Municipal Government for approval and filed with the Ministry of Education.

Local Nango, Tungda, Chungda

Alumni Association Meeting Today

Notes from Knocking on the Ancient Temple Bell (10) (9)

The Reclusive Husband Who Doesn't Remove the Courtyard Grass

Twenty-three

When the villagers heard that a new teacher had arrived, men, women, old, and young all came to see, as lively as watching a new groom. We introduced each of them to Mr. Zhu. Mr. Zhu immediately gathered the children together and said, "Children, let me tell you a story. Once upon a time, there was a farmer who only took care of planting fields for others, leaving his own field barren. Later, he had no rice to eat and starved to death. At the time of his death, a bird suddenly landed on the corner of the roof and chirped 'Cuckoo, cuckoo.' Since then, villagers have believed that this cuckoo bird is the old farmer who starved to death, calling on people every day to 'Cuckoo' to avoid starvation. You must have already known this story. But do you know what the cuckoo bird's chirping actually means? What it says is:

'Cuckoo cuckoo, Hurry up and cuckoo. If you don't cuckoo, No rice to cook porridge. If you want to cook porridge, Hurry up and cuckoo. Cuckoo cook porridge, Cook porridge cuckoo.'

'Let's all say it together, and we have to say it quickly and correctly. Whoever says it the best, I will give this little leather ball to him to manage.'

Everyone was very happy to recite. Wang Er's sister-in-law's youngest son, Ying'er, recited the fastest, without missing a single word. He was as happy as a living immortal and took on the responsibility of managing this little leather ball. Mr. Zhu then began to teach the children to pat this strange and fun thing. Even the older farmers had never seen this little ball, and some joined the children's ranks to pat it a couple of times, saying with a smile, 'This thing is fun!'"

The Shanghai Branch of the Local Nango, Tungda, Chungda Alumni Association will hold a meeting at 11:00 AM today on the ninth floor of the Eight Immortals Bridge YMCA in the French Concession, and a gathering will also be held. It is reported that there are more than one hundred members of the association. It is feared that a few students have not been investigated in detail for this meeting, so when issuing the meeting notice, all members are requested to invite familiar classmates to attend the meeting so that everyone can attend and enjoy each other's company.

Grass Court Tennis Club News

The Venue Problem for the Mixed Tournament. Moreover, the courts of the French Chamber of Commerce, except for the Grass Court Tennis Club's special agreement to borrow them, cannot be used for temporary borrowing for matches. In the future, all kinds of matches of the Grass Court Tennis Club will be handled in this way. Shocking News | World Games

The Puppet State is Actually Allowed to Send Athletes to Participate

Resolution of the Preparatory Committee on May 28 | Citing Previous Examples of the Philippines and India

Japan Reportedly Selected Yu Xiwei | Will Our Country Protest?

What are the Feelings of the Chinese People?

The 10th World Games will be held in Los Angeles, USA, starting on the 30th of next month. More than 50 countries will participate, as reported previously. Recently, shocking news has come that the members of the Games Organizing Committee actually approved the selection of athletes from the Manchurian Puppet State to participate on May 28. Shen Siliang, honorary director of the National Sports Association, solemnly declared that he cannot attend without his signature. Manchuria is Chinese territory, and now the flag of the Puppet State will be wavering in the Games field. Will our country's authorities rise up to protest?

Preparatory Committee Approves Puppet State Participation

As the date of the Games is approaching and representatives from various countries are arriving in the United States one after another, the reception committee of the Games is extremely busy, and the Olympic Village is in a state of tension. The organizing committee of the Games held its 29th plenary staff meeting on the night of May 28. The number of countries currently registered to participate is 51, with approximately 2,000 athletes, excluding team leaders and coaches. The previous Amsterdam Games had 46 participating countries. This year, both the number of countries and the number of people have broken all previous records. The only member country that has not sent athletes to participate is China. Most surprisingly, the Games actually decided to recognize the Manchurian Puppet State's participation in the Games and approved the Puppet State's participation on the grounds of previous examples of the Philippines and India. The Philippines and India are not independent countries recognized by the world but have already obtained the right to participate in the Games' group military position. Therefore, the Games disregarded China's sovereign control over Manchuria and simply allowed its participation. It is hoped that the Chinese people will quickly find a way to drive the Manchurian flag out of Los Angeles.

Full Text of the Games Resolution Record

The meeting record of the Games meeting on the night of May 28 is recorded below. (1) After the end of this Games, the Anglo-American International Athletics Championships will be held in San Francisco on August 14.

(2) The Japanese delegation entrusted this Games to contact the German delegation on its behalf to hold the Japan-Germany International Athletics Championships in San Francisco. It was resolved to start contacting Germany immediately.

(3) In addition to previously registering to participate in field hockey, India has now added registration to participate in track and field and swimming. It was resolved to allow them to participate.

(4) The "Manchurian government" entrusted the Japanese delegation to register with this Games on its behalf to send two athletes to participate in track and field. It was resolved to allow the country to join in accordance with the previous examples of India and the Philippines participating in this Games.

Will Yu Xiwei Be a Representative?

To Be Confirmed

According to the Puppet State's Shuntian Gongbao, the athlete sent by the Puppet State to participate in the World Games is a certain Yu from Andong County, who recently won the 800-meter race (hosted by the Puppet State) in the Liaoning Provincial Games, with a score of 2 minutes and 2.2 seconds. Japanese newspapers widely reported that this person is Yu Xiwei, but whether this is true remains to be verified.

Yugoslavia Will Not Participate

Belgrade, Yugoslavia, 10th. The technical committee of the Yugoslavia Sokol Sports Association has confirmed that it will not participate in the World Games held in Los Angeles, USA.

Business News

Finance

Call Loan Rate Rebounds Slightly

Yesterday, the call loan rate seemed to rebound slightly. The morning market rate was two li, or 6 qian, 9 fen, 2 li, and a half. The afternoon market softened by 0.125 to 6 qian, 9 fen, 2 li, 3 hao, and 7 hu and a half. Gold Price Without Major Fluctuations

Not Exceeding Four Tael Spread

Yesterday, after several days of rising gold prices, there was a reaction, and the market showed a sluggish trend. The market was quite calm, and from morning to noon, the price spread did not exceed four taels. In the end, there was a slight drop of a few cents. The cash flow of different firms varied, with most selling off and short sellers buying. Market sentiment seemed weak. Although the silver market fell, it was not considered significant, and the opening price was low. Subsequently, the market fluctuated, but foreign exchange tended to stabilize, and the final price was just over 724 taels. The market will be closed next Saturday. This week, although there were no major changes, the market was in a state of consolidation. Initially, large gold bars continued to rise, but downstream demand decreased, resulting in a low price of 711 taels and 8 mace. However, spot goods were scarce, especially as a certain bank showed active trading. Therefore, the longs sought to exploit the situation and raised the swap rate. The market price gradually advanced, frequently rising by more than ten taels, and reached a high price of 729 taels by Friday. Afterwards, the Kwong Syndicate sold off, leading to a softening trend. Overall, the total increase for the week was 17 taels and some change, up 9 taels and 1 mace compared to last Saturday. A Bird's-Eye View of the New York Stock Market This Week

Report from American Eastern Bank

The New York stock market this week, after the continuous rise at the end of last week, initially showed a reactive decline. However, shortly after the passage of the bonus case and the unemployment relief case, merchants inevitably developed a sense of aversion, fearing that the national budget would still not be able to maintain balance. Therefore, the stock market continued to fall, not far from the lowest record. Fortunately, industrial stocks were able to stand firm when they were half a point away from the low, and by Friday, famous securities stocks were able to compete fiercely. The Oppenheim Motors stock rose by more than 21 points in one day. This extreme advance was due to a large number of short-covering.

The business situation this week was also very good. The freight tonnage of the iron and steel industry was more than last week, and the American wheat situation was also good. According to the Department of Agriculture's statistics, last year's winter harvest was 14,660,000, a low figure not seen since 1925. Automobile production increased by 3,000 vehicles compared to last week, but the news from the steel industry was not good. Looking at the situation from all sides, there has been definite progress recently. According to general opinion, the decline in the New York stock market is already far beyond the general business situation. Therefore, after the government's finances are rectified, the stock market will definitely improve. The Dow Jones index for this week is attached on the left:

Yarn and Cotton

The Yarn Market is Declining Daily

The cotton yarn market is showing signs of failure. Due to the high base price of local yarn and the cheapness of raw materials, the price of cotton yarn itself is low. Furthermore, the domestic socio-economic situation is depressed, rural areas are bankrupt, and the people are impoverished. As a result, actual sales are stagnant, and world commodity prices are falling sharply, reaching unprecedented lows. Therefore, Japanese merchants are selling yarn everywhere, engaging in intense competition. North China is being filled with their yarn, which is severely impacting the local yarn market. Comparing the price of local yarn with the world market, it is uniquely high, so how can the yarn market be maintained? Fortunately, the factories in Shanghai that stockpile goods do not have large inventories, so yarn prices are temporarily higher than cotton prices. The most important key factor is the actual demand for cotton.

The Selling of Cotton via Public Bidding is Not Over

The opening of the market before public bidding was stable as foreign cotton prices rebounded. However, the price of the far-term futures contract declined, and the price of each month’s contracts (2nd, 3rd, 4th) declined by 5-6-7-8 cents as the raw cotton price declined. The market sentiment was weaker in the afternoon, and the selling pressure was high, with the prices of each month’s contracts declining by 5–7 cents. The total volume of the transactions throughout the day was 12,300 bales. The selling companies and volume of bales were as follows: 850 bales for Suilong, 1350 bales for Rongxing, 700 bales for Xiesheng, 1250 bales for Xincheng, 850 bales for Yichang, 550 bales for Dachangcheng. The buying companies and volume of bales were as follows: 800 bales for Tongyu, 950 bales for Tianlong, 750 bales for Yicheng, 850 bales for Yongda, 500 bales for Yuantai, and 400 bales for Changfeng. Currently, with the gloomy global situation, the American Eastern Cotton Company, the Shanghai branch of the US Cotton Exchange, was canvassing in the market, offering Mitter M2 at 27 taels, with 10,000 bales available, with a rebate of 1 tael still possible. This cotton can be used to produce 20-count yarn. However, Shin Yick Factory, mindful of the sluggish global trend, dared not purchase it. But compared to foreign cotton, the price level of local cotton was still far apart.

Silk and Tea

Dantu's New Cocoon Shipments Are Not Smooth

Cocoon Prices Too Low, Silkworm Costs Not Covered

Most Is Self-Dried, Reeled, and Sold as Silk

In various towns and villages in Dantu, the spring silkworm farming has been greatly reduced this year. In addition, the weather has been unfavorable, silkworm diseases are rampant, and many leaves have been shed. The cocoon production is extremely low, and the cocoon markets have few shops for rent. Only local silk manufacturers are setting up scales to limit the purchase of cocoons. The purchase prices are very low. The highest price for improved breeds is 24-25 yuan lower. Silkworm farmers cannot cover their costs and mostly dry and reel the silk themselves, waiting for the opportune time to sell the raw silk. Therefore, the export of dry cocoons is not smooth, and the cocoon market has ended. The statistics for dry cocoons loaded onto the Beijing-Shanghai trains bound for Wuxi and Shanghai are only 500-600 bales.

There Is Already a Move to Purchase Bud-Plucked Special Tea

The purchase of bud-plucked special tea from Wudong and Dunxi has already been initiated by Ruichang and Dued Firms. However, the opening market price is 160-170 taels, 110-120 taels lower than last year. The selling price is extremely low, and therefore, Chinese tea merchants have already sent out large numbers of telegrams, notifying the stoppage of the purchase of this bud-plucked special tea. However, although the sales of ordinary special tea have slightly improved, the sentiment among various firms varies, and the market is still feared to decline rather than rise. Green teas such as needle-eyebrow and fine-eyebrow are still being sold as soon as they arrive, and there is no large stagnation of pearl tea. Ewo Foreign Firm has changed its approach to observing the situation of black tea from Qifu and other areas. Other firms have not seen much improvement in sales, and the market has significantly weakened compared to before.

Wutun Tea Market Brief Report

Wuyuan Tea Prices Difficult to Lower: This year's new tea from Wuyuan has seen a reduction in production volume. When the mountain households harvested their tea gardens, tea merchants rushed to buy it up. Only about one-third of the goods in the market remain unsold. Although sales in the Shanghai market are sluggish, and telegrams from warehouses are pessimistic, the mountain households are unwilling to immediately lower prices due to the high prices they previously sold at. The opening price for the Jiangwan and Gangtou markets in eastern Wuyuan is still required to be 80 yuan. The Enkou Tea Firm bought the reclaimed tea from Wukou in northern Wuyuan at a price of 64 yuan, which is not much different from the initial market price. Various firms, seeing these subsequent developments and the difficulty in lowering mountain prices, are mostly adopting a cautious approach and delaying purchases due to the poor Shanghai market.

Zhangshan Tea Harvesting and Production is Nearing Completion: Zhangshan Yunwu Tea in northern Wuyuan, due to its location on high cliffs and colder climate, develops more slowly than tea from the mountain plains. Every year, it must wait until the new tea from the entire county is on the market before it can begin harvesting. This year's weather in the mountains is even colder, and tea buds have sprouted even more slowly. According to farmers in the mountains, the new tea from this mountain has already begun to be harvested and produced a week ago. Due to sufficient labor, it will soon be completed. The quality and aroma of the tea are better than in previous years. However, affected by the sluggish Shanghai market, none of the past customers have yet come to the mountain to discuss prices.

Tunxi Tea Prices Are Increasingly Lower: After receiving news of the unfavorable Shanghai market situation, Tunxi's tea firms have significantly reduced the amount of tea they are buying. Although the source of tea arriving in recent days is gradually increasing, there are still few inquiries, and the market price has fallen from 80 yuan to 50 yuan. If the Shanghai market does not improve, most firms plan to complete one batch and then end the season to avoid losses.

Grain: The Riverbank Rice Market Drops Another Ten Cents

South Shanghai: Yesterday's rice market had over 30 rice dealers in the neighborhood and around 130 rice dealers in total, including those from the pier. The trading in the main street was not good. North Geng and Central Geng rice were each down by ten cents. The early and late rice markets were sluggish, but fortunately, there was not much cargo. The market price followed and shortened by ten cents. The Yanglu pointed rice was scarce, and the market situation was weak. The fermented rice had few stocks, and the situation stabilized.

Xinzha: Yesterday's early arrival market had a slight amount of early market trading, but it was very slow. In the afternoon, the unloading of rice on the riverbank was quite good. The price of thin rice decreased by ten cents at the opening of the market. Changxi North Geng rice was stable, and the quality was inferior. The Yanglu pointed rice and fermented rice were scarce and firm. In the two markets before and after, about 3,000 shi of rice were unloaded at the riverbank.

Foreign Rice Falls in the Morning, Stabilizes in the Evening

Jiangbei Syndicate Continues to Load

Various Rice Types Decreased by a Little Over Ten Cents

Yesterday's foreign rice market situation: In the morning, following the tired wind of continuous days, the situation was very weak, and all rice types decreased by a little over ten cents. In the afternoon, the weather turned cloudy, and the market sentiment rebounded. The Jiangbei Syndicate and the villages in this area began to buy, and the market recovered and stabilized. However, the stock on the market was sufficient, and foreign firms continued to canvass for business. If there were no large syndicate purchases, it would be very difficult for the market price to rebound. A total of 3,000 bags of small Jiaomi rice were offered, priced at 10.04 yuan to 10.025 yuan. There were also 250 bags of old coarse rice, priced at 9.15 yuan. There were 500 bags of Kolarady coarse rice, priced at 9.37 yuan. There were 100 bags of Saigon No. 1, priced at 11.6 yuan. Also, new Jiangxi Jiyuan rice continued to arrive, with 150 bags offered, priced at 13.5 yuan. Except for the Jiangbei Syndicate asking about the small Jiaomi rice, all the others were purchased by the local village.

Flour Market in Quiet Strength

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, each contract seemed to turn calm. Because the quoted price of foreign wheat rebounded by about 3-5 cents, the opening price was higher than the previous day by 0.01 yuan. However, by the third session, the buying interest was quiet again, and the market softened. Until the opening of the market in the afternoon, the large factories held their ground and showed no intention of releasing flour. In addition, the weather was unfavorable, with a high probability of rain, so although the transactions were scarce, the market atmosphere was quite stable. Observing the future, actual sales must improve and factory flour must have an outlet before there is hope. The final result was that the July contract was better than the previous day by 0.0125 yuan, the August contract was better by 0.01 yuan, the September contract was better by 0.0125 yuan, the October contract was better by 0.017 yuan, and the November contract was better by 0.015 yuan.

Cereal Market Remained Dull

Yesterday, the cereal market opened in the morning, and various market conditions showed a sluggish trend again. Although foreign wheat was quoted higher by thirty-five cents, due to the continuous arrival of new wheat from the mainland and the potential actions of Shanghai factories, mainland manufacturers were mostly observing. Under these circumstances, they were inevitably extremely passive. The price for July was as low as three taels, two maces, and eight fen, and for August, three taels and three maces and five fen, which shows the depression of the cereal market. When the afternoon session opened, it was initially flat, but later, as the flour market improved slightly, people's sentiment was also lifted. However, transactions remained stagnant, making development difficult. As a result, July decreased by two fen compared to the previous day, August decreased by one fen, September remained unchanged, October increased by one fen, and November remained unchanged. There were transactions of foreign wheat from the Hankou group, with Canadian No. 3 wheat at three taels and seven maces and five fen for delivery in Hankou. Local factories offered three taels and six maces, and negotiations were still ongoing.

North-South Goods: Abundant Harvest of Sea Mouth Branches

New Products to Arrive Within Two Weeks

Last year, Sea Mouth branches had a poor harvest, with no kernels available. Now, after extremes, a bountiful year has come. According to reports, this year's new goods are expected to be about 70% of the norm. They are expected to arrive in Shanghai within about half a month. Because the harvest is abundant, the cost will naturally be lower, so the market price is bound to be low.

Metals: Yellow Brass Coins – Extreme Stillness Breeds Movement

The yellow brass coin market had previously been very sluggish due to tight money conditions and the cessation of operations by various groups, causing sales to be under downward pressure. In recent days, the Hankou and Fujian groups have had demand, so the market is thriving due to the need for transactions, leading to a sense of movement from extreme stillness. The standard price has also risen sharply, estimated at thirty-eight taels per dan.

Free Talk

Two-One Branch Talk

The Prophecy of the Poem "The Sun of the East"

— Shan Liao

The two chapters of the poem "The Sun of the East" in the "Airs of Qi" of the Book of Songs, the small preface says it is a poem of satire against decline. When I was a child, I read these two chapters of poetry, read them casually, and had no feelings. Now, when I reread it, I can't help but be shocked! These two chapters of poetry do not seem to be poems satirizing decline two thousand years ago, but rather modern maxims to spur the people! If you don't believe me, I'll write out the original poem of "Airs of Qi" first:

"The sun of the east! That beautiful maiden, is in my room! Is in my room, treads to me! The sun of the east! That beautiful maiden, is at my door! Is at my door, treads to my hair!" I only need to slightly tamper with it, changing the character for beautiful "shu" to the character for dwarf "zhuru"; changing the character for treads "lǚ" to the character for management "lǐ"; then, these two chapters of poetry become stimulating

mottos!

"The sun of the east! That dwarfish child, is in my room! Is in my room, manages me immediately! The sun of the east! That dwarfish child, is at my door! Is at my door, manages my hair!" The first chapter says that the dwarfs of the East have already entered our room! Having entered the room, then managing us is about to begin! Therefore, the poem says: "Manages me immediately!"

The second chapter says that the dwarfs of the East have already entered our door; having entered the door, then managing us has the opportunity to begin, so the poem says: "Manages my hair!"

Where is the room? Shanghai is the room.

Where is the door? The three northeastern provinces are the door.

On September 18th, the dwarfish child entered my door, managing us, the opportunity has begun.

On January 28th, the dwarfish child entered my room, managing us, is about to begin.

All patriotic youths of the world, every morning, read "The Sun of the East" three hundred times, the merit is immeasurable!

The Poet's Room

— Yingge

丨Miscellaneous Writings of the Old Capital, Nine丨

Please forgive me, I cannot tell you the poet's name, because he is still alive now, and he still needs to do some things for his life. If I were to write his name, it would more or less affect his

life; I feel unbearable in my heart. But I can tell you, he has a very unique name, and you will call out in surprise when you know it.

The poet came from a famous mountain half a month ago, twirling his yellow cane. Since settling in a corner of our courtyard, we haven't seen the poet's face all day long. Naturally, he went outside to look for his poetry. At night, when people have already fallen asleep in bed, the dogs barked, and at the same time, our poet returned. Apart from the clear "clack-clack" of his leather shoes hitting your brain, you only hear the poet humming lines of poetry in a long voice. Naturally, this is the only quatrain the poet found after a day's work.

The poet's hair is very long, black and thick, draped over his shoulders. His complexion? Needless to say, it is also very pale. When you see him, you might think he is a living ghost. And his room? It is also different from others. One day, the old maid was mopping the floor of the poet's room, and she called out seriously, "Master Zhou! Come and see." For a moment, I was called by her and ran over out of curiosity. Sure enough, our poet's room did not disappoint us. Let's see 丨the floor in the room was dug up in two large pieces, planted with two oleander bushes. The oleanders could not receive rain and dew in the room and were withered; yes, only withering is poetic. There is no table or chair in the room. The only piece of furniture is a short and long plank bed, which is what supports my poet's body every night. The floor is piled with books and paper, and the old maid has tried several times to move them out, but the poet has stopped her. I picked up a copy of Xue Lai's Selected Poems from the ground and opened it. I couldn't read it at all! It turned out that these precious poems had become the dance floor for bedbugs. Looking at the white walls again, they were full of the poet's masterpieces, the most touching of which were the two lines "Mary and I, traveling to Dedicate." The old maid asked me! "What exactly does this gentleman do?" I told her very honestly; "He is a poet." "Corpse man"? The old maid didn't understand.

World Small Chronicles

— Haike

Not only women but also many men love to use cosmetics such as perfume and soap. For example, former British King George IV spent 700 pounds a year on cosmetics. If calculated at the current market price, it amounts to as much as 2,000 pounds.

In Maine, USA, there is a Hill family. The children are all seven in number. Mr. Hill's father was one of seven children and also had seven sons. Mr. Hill is one of them. After marrying his wife, he also successively had seven sons. The eldest son has long been married and has also had seven sons.

Men, women, and children throughout England love sweets. According to the statistics for the most recent year, it reached as much as 750 million pounds. If the population is taken as a proportion, the average person eats 17 pounds per year. ▲There are several old shops in London. There are 650 that are more than 100 years old. There are also several that are even older and have hundreds of years of history.

Strange Taste

— Yang Yixiao

Huai'an cattail shoots and eel are available in all seasons. Cattail shoots are produced in Huai'an Shaohu Lake. Those who work in this industry on Lianhua Street are lined up like the teeth of a comb. The taste is the freshest and most tender. It is suitable for both meat and vegetarian dishes. Eel produced in the fields is said to be the best. Huai cuisine has unique cooking methods that are beyond the reach of ordinary people. It is said that Huai chefs can make a full feast with eel. The forms and flavors are different. The so-called cattail shoots and eel are unique to Jianghuai.

Jinan cuisine has pre-rain shrimp kernels, which taste excellent. The method is to use a bowl of raw shrimp meat, and another egg, remove the yolk and use the white. Beat it thoroughly. Take a handful of pre-rain tea leaves and mix them evenly with the shrimp kernels, so that they can be separated individually to a suitable degree. Add a little salt. Heat the lard wok. When the oil is boiling, use a colander to hold the shrimp kernels evenly. Put them into the wok and stir-fry two or three times, then remove them. The tea leaves have already been released, with a clear fragrance and sweetness, and are quite flavorful.

Miscellaneous Notes from Wuxia

— Kill

The flower affairs in Jinchang have long been known for their allure. Although they suffered a blow during the Qingbai transition, it wasn't long before those who asked about the wailing of the people once again filled the hotels. However, at a time when all industries are declining, the life among the flowers is also very bleak. Now, times create heroes. These roadside willows and wallflowers have all taken advantage of the east wind and flown to other branches. Tens of thousands of gold bells are protecting them as they leave as mistresses. Even those who remain have seen their prices soar, no longer waiting to be sold without anyone caring as they once were.

The Nineteenth Route Army's resistance against Japan is the key to the survival of our Republic of China. All Chinese citizens should share the enemy's hatred and unite in providing assistance to fight for the survival of the nation. However, when the Nineteenth Route Army shed blood in Shanghai, the funds collected by our Wuhou Fang Service Group in Wujun, a city of 300,000 residents, to assist the soldiers at the front only amounted to more than 6,000 gold, while the losses suffered by those who fled to other places and were robbed by lake bandits often exceeded 10,000 gold. The lack of national consciousness among our people and the self-preservation of the wealthy are truly enough to make those with a heart cry and sigh.

On Thrift and Frugality to Save the Nation (8)

— Narrated by Nie Zengjifen, Written by His Son Qijie

Modern people like to show off their own opinions, confusing right and wrong. Most people use their ears as eyes and cannot make choices. As a result, they despise etiquette and destroy sacred words, feeling pleased with themselves. This has created today's phenomenon of poverty, chaos, danger, and urgency. Who knows that all the disputes in the world have been personally experienced and studied by ancient philosophers? From the effects of their actions, they issued accurate conclusions. Following these conclusions will solve all economic problems and class disputes. Judging by the latest theories of socialism, they are mostly suitable, and the more the world evolves, the more their appropriateness becomes apparent. However, this is beyond the scope of this article, so I will not discuss it in detail. I only want to contribute my personal experiences and lessons to those who are responsible for guiding society in this era, hoping that they will give it serious consideration. If a large number of prominent figures set an example, turn the tide, not lightly regard national customs and value European customs, and practice what Dayu and other famous sages who built the nation in ancient times did, which is to hate fine clothing, meager food, and humble palaces, promote simple and crude domestic products, and collectively regard the use of luxurious, exquisite, and convenient imported goods as shameful, the effect can be seen immediately in the blink of an eye. However, in today's society, women have a greater influence on trends than men, and their responsibility is even greater. Therefore, I especially hope that our women can see this first. Wives encourage their husbands, mothers encourage their sons, and sisters encourage their brothers, all sacrificing their personal desires and working together to save the nation with thrift and frugality, to save the people, to not deceive the crowd and to be harmonious with the masses. If we can achieve this within five years, national defense will be secure. National defense is not just about strong walls, deep moats, and sharp weapons. Guanzi said, "Etiquette, righteousness, integrity, and shame are the four pillars of a nation. If the four pillars are not upheld, the nation will perish." Mencius said that a city with high walls, deep moats, strong soldiers, and sharp armor will be abandoned if the four pillars are not upheld. The late Duke Wen said, "I am not deeply worried about the lack of soldiers, and I do not cry bitterly about the lack of rations." But looking at this world, it is impossible to quickly find someone who does not prioritize personal gain, who fears to be behind in upholding righteousness, and who has unwavering loyalty and indignation. This is truly something to sigh about.

The day of national demise is not far off.

The memorial service for the martyrs and compatriots who died in the Shanghai Anti-Japanese War was held in Wuxia. Contemporary great men arrived one after another. The order of the meeting place was maintained by soldiers of the Sixtieth Division and the Sea Scouts. The security was strict. The park and the public sports ground were completely designated as special security zones. Anyone who was not a soldier, policeman, or had a guest pass was not allowed to stop and visit. When the great men entered the meeting place, they were welcomed into the city by horse-drawn carriages hired by the meeting. For a time, the vehicles on May 30th Road were lined up, creating a strange sight. In the past, Li Hanqiu of Jiangdu wrote the novel "Guangling Tide," which had a section about horse-drawn carriages entering the city to the Yuanmiao Temple. Readers criticized him for not being familiar with the situation in Wuxia. Now, Li's prediction has become a reality. If he knew in the afterlife, he would boast of being a prophet.

The mourning couplets and sacrifices sent from various places to the memorial service for the martyrs and compatriots who died in the Shanghai Anti-Japanese War were piled up like mountains. Among them, the wax-made wreath sent by the Northeastern soldiers was colorful and eye-catching. The two rifles and one bomb seized from the Japanese invaders, presented by all the soldiers of a certain division, were made into the most unique flower screen. On the day of the meeting, the mourning couplets were hung all around the meeting place and the park, and the eyes were filled with white. There were many touching words among them. This day of mourning may slightly comfort the heroic souls of the martyrs. However, the Northeast has fallen, and Liaoji has not been recovered. The restoration of the homeland still depends on the soldiers who have not died, following the blood path of the martyrs to advance.

Among the universities destroyed in the war zone, Jinan University is truly one of the luckiest. Although a part of the Science Museum was bombed,

Record of Double Life in Military Service (76)

— Master of Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter Nine: A Fictitious Alarm of Being Evicted on a Special Train, Sitting in a Cold Government Office Turns into a Distant Fantasy

When An Yutian saw Xiao Mao, it was like seeing a relative in times of distress. He was overjoyed beyond words. But when he asked about what happened last night, he was still full of anger. He replied resentfully, "Don't mention it. That fellow surnamed Guo didn't follow through and actually sent me to the guard car, where I suffered all night." As he spoke, he remembered the insults he had suffered and stopped himself from saying more, fearing he would lose face if he told the whole story. He changed the subject and asked where the ladies were now. Mao Deshun said, "Alas, who knew that little rascal was trying to save trouble and sent you to that kind of place? That car was separated by seven or eight cars. No wonder I couldn't find you. Now the Fifth Madam has returned to the yamen. Your Madam is worried and is still waiting in the waiting room, waiting for you to move to the First Guesthouse together. We already sent a telegram from the car to reserve the rooms." After speaking, he hurriedly pulled him to the first-class waiting room. When Liang Xiaoyun suddenly saw that his spirit had declined to this extent in just one night, she couldn't help but ask him in detail. He repeatedly shook his head and sighed, only saying that it was not too late to talk about it at the hotel. After Mao Deshun sent them to the First Guesthouse and took his leave, he told Liang Xiaoyun the whole story in detail, and even complained that she hadn't sent someone to look for him everywhere when he got on the train. Liang Xiaoyun clicked her tongue and only laughed, "How dare you? A dignified man, traveling with his wife, and I have to take care of and bring all the luggage and servants for you. You don't care about anything and still complain that I don't take care of you. Are you still three or two years old, and do I have to hold you in my arms? Learn a lesson from this. It's your own fault for being so inexperienced.

You just followed people in a daze without even turning back to tell me first. That's why you made such a big joke. I advise you to discuss things with me before you do anything in the future. Don't be so reckless. There are many things you don't understand in this officialdom." An Yutian, having been taught this lesson, also realized that it was his own fault and didn't say much more. He didn't expect that after staying in this hotel, he received a call from Mao Deshun that night, saying that Military Governor Ye had set off again to inspect troops elsewhere and would not be back for three to five days, telling them to wait patiently. From then on, An Yutian waited quietly, but Liang Xiaoyun was called by the Fifth Madam every day, either by phone or by sending someone to pick her up at the yamen to play, leaving An Yutian alone in the hotel during the day feeling very lonely. On the sixth day, Liang Xiaoyun actually played mahjong in the yamen all night and didn't return. An Yutian heard everyone in the hotel spreading the word that Military Governor Ye had returned.
