Sick Woman

Dies from Shock Caused by Fire

Careless Boiling of Medicine Causes Fire in Shack

Police Station Forbids Rebuilding of Shacks

Yesterday at around 1:00 AM, the shack of Yao Zhenlai, a native of Jiangbei living in the West Garbage Pond of Yangjia Ferry in Pudong, caught fire because Yao's wife, Chen, was ill and Yao was boiling medicine. Unexpectedly, the charcoal fire shot out, and the bamboo rafters and thatched tiles caught fire immediately. Yao and his son rushed out in panic, but Yao's wife, Chen, collapsed on the bed due to shock and died. The police officers of the First Section of the Third District dragged her out and found that she seemed to have shattered her courage and there was no way to revive her. At that time, the fire spread outward and was very fierce. The fire was then extinguished by the nearby Rongchang Match Factory, which drew water from a pavilion to put out the fire. The fire burned for about an hour, destroying a total of nine shacks and partially destroying two at both ends. Afterwards, Yao Zhenlai, the person who started the fire, saw that his house was destroyed and his wife was dead. He believed that he had caused a great disaster and feared that he would be arrested and punished by the authorities, so he fled with his son without a trace. Yang Zhongquan, the chief of the First Section of the Third District, instructed the local guards to report to the local court to examine the body of Yao's wife. He also issued a notice stating that shacks are most prone to fire, and that all shacks must not be rebuilt to avoid repeating the mistake of the past. The notice reads: "For the purpose of issuing a notice, it is hereby noted that the addition of shacks is not allowed. It has been repeatedly ordered by the Public Security Bureau to strictly prohibit it. Recently, it was found that the West Garbage Pond unfortunately suffered a fire last night. All shacks that were burned and removed must not be rebuilt to prevent fire hazards. This notice is hereby issued to all shack dwellers for compliance. Those who dare to violate this order will be summoned and investigated. Do not say that you were not warned."

The Sauce and Wine Industry Receives a Ministry Directive

The Association of Sauce and Wine Stores previously submitted a request to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to send a telegram to the Jiangsu Stamp and Tobacco Tax Bureau and the Central Ministry of Finance to investigate the case of the Shanghai Local Yellow Wine Tax Collection Branch forcibly raising the prices of goods and arbitrarily changing the tax system. The industry received a directive from the Ministry of Finance yesterday, which reads: "Directive No. 364 of the Ministry of Finance, Seal: A document from the Shanghai Association of Sauce and Wine Stores, stating that Lin Xitao, Director of the Shanghai Local Yellow Wine Tax Collection Branch of the Jiangsu Stamp and Tobacco Tax Bureau, coerced merchants and abused his power. I implore you to investigate and dismiss him from his post and hold him accountable to quell public anger and maintain political integrity. I have received your request. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce has also sent a telegram requesting investigation. I have also ordered the Jiangsu Stamp and Tobacco Tax Bureau to send personnel to investigate whether Lin Xitao, Director of the Shanghai Local Yellow Wine Tax Collection Branch, has indeed engaged in extortion and harassment by taking advantage of his position, and to report the facts for review. You are hereby notified."

French Water and Electricity Company

Establishment of the Mutual Benefit Society for Staff of the Transportation Department

The more than 1,000 employees of the French Water and Electricity Company in this city, including the inspectors, ticket collectors, ticket writers, railroad staff, lantern lighters, track repairers, management office staff, ticket office staff, driver department, and ticket sales department, recognizing the importance of organizing a group, initiated the organization of the "Shanghai French Water and Electricity Company Transportation Department Staff Mutual Benefit Society" by Li Linshu and others. The organization was approved by the Municipal Party Headquarters and has been preparing for several months. The inaugural meeting was held at the association's office at No. 244 Kaizier Road (intersection of Songshan Road) in the French Concession at 9:00 AM on the 9th. Representatives were gathered and Li Linshu, Yan Yunjin, Cai Hongjun, Yin Yichun, Liu Degong, Pan Changlin, Zhao Fuming, Qian Jinyuan, Zhong Runsheng, Chen Bangjun, Pu Huailin, and others were elected as directors. Wang Jun, Zhao Fuxian, Lu Hairong, Bao Anchang, Zhang Wenhong, and others were elected as alternate directors. Gu Yingchun, Ren Liansheng, Liu Yanxiu, Pang Guiqing, Liu Yanmou, Zhang Yilu, Dai Huanmin, and others were elected as supervisors. Qiu Songshan, Yan Chengfu, Wang Helin, and others were elected as alternate supervisors. The establishment was announced on the same day. Zhou Lianze was sent by the Party Headquarters to attend and provide guidance. Zhang Zhuozai was sent by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to attend and supervise the election. There was much encouragement for the establishment of the association. It is said that after the establishment of the association, the first public welfare project will be to establish a cooperative for the consumption of food by the members, in order to reduce the financial burden on the members.

Message from the Reorganization Committee of the Chinese Friendship Association

Publication of Letter to Members

A letter from the Reorganization Committee of the Chinese Friendship Association of the Shanghai French Concession Municipal Council to the members reads: "To all members: We have been ordered by the Municipal Party Headquarters to organize the Reorganization Committee and assume the important mission of continuing the unfinished work of the first Executive Supervisory Committee and seeking welfare for all our members. On the one hand, we should indeed do our best to fulfill our aspirations and responsibilities. On the other hand, we hope that all members who are also in dire straits can unite together to jointly shoulder this arduous task and urge us at the same time. Before starting the reorganization, we felt the various misfortunes of the past, so we have the following points to ask all members to pay close attention to: (1) Our thinking should be scientific and our actions should be disciplined. We must avoid making unreasonable remarks and irregular actions. (2) Our spirits should be full, our attitude should be relaxed, our vision should be broad, and our minds should be clear. We must not commit the various ills of depression, confusion, short-sightedness, and confusion. (3) We must absolutely abide by and obey the association's constitution and all orders, and we must love the association so that life becomes collectivized. (4) We must do our best in our personal professional duties and must not have various bad habits such as perfunctoriness and laziness. The above four points are the first points that we need to warn all members to pay attention to. In the future, we can contribute our opinions at any time to consolidate the foundation of the association and reach the realm of development, so that we can complete our responsibilities. Internal rectification is our only way out. All problems depend on the results of the rectification. Members, let us strive forward. Reorganization Committee: Qiu Gaogang, Sun Shanhai, Mao Dekang, Shen Caigeng, Zhao Ziyun, Zhang Jinbao, Ding Youzhi, Pan Wenqing, Wang Yaogen. June 10, 21st year."

Recent News of Refugee Factory

Since the refugee factory founded by the Chinese People's Livelihood Improvement Society rented a house in Beixinjing and actively carried out its work, it has been highly praised by the society. The Shanghai Citizens' Local Maintenance Association recently transferred the work equipment, materials, and educational supplies of the Nanyuan Refugee Vocational Training Center to the factory for expansion. The remaining 20-odd refugees were also accommodated by the factory. The Ningbo Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai donated 30 canvas beds and 30 quilts to the factory. The Overseas Chinese Federation donated 29 bags of rice. Various groups and individuals have visited the factory one after another to express their appreciation. The factory's hosiery department previously borrowed 10 hosiery machines from the Sanjin Hosiery Factory in the South City. Now, the Hongxing Hosiery Factory has enthusiastically lent 15 more hosiery machines. In the future, production can be further expanded. The society has now organized a Refugee Factory Committee, inviting Xiang Kangyuan, Pan Yangyao, Huang Jingwan, Shi Jiuyun, Pan Jishi, Qian Zhenya, Yang Chonggao, and Chen Shudong to be members to plan everything. The Standing Committee of the Society's Board of Directors has resolved to invite Honorary Secretary-General Zhu Maocheng to concurrently serve as the Director of the Refugee Factory to preside over the work.

A Gang of Thugs Extort Mr. Zhang Shangyi

Seven Letters Sent with Threatening Language

Intended to Extort Five Thousand Dollars

Detectives Intercept and Arrest Three Men

Mr. Zhang Shangyi, the Chinese Chief Inspector of the Public Concession, residing at No. 123 Chengdu Road, has successively received seven threatening letters from a gang of bandits using the name Li Jianhong, starting last month and continuing until the end of this month. The letters contained violent language and intended to extort five thousand dollars. Zhang reported the letters to the police station and requested an investigation. The day before yesterday morning, Zhang received another phone call from the gang, scheduling a meeting at 5:20 PM in front of the Exchange Building on Avenue Edward VII, and requested a representative to bring the money with a copy of the Dalu Daily as a sign. Zhang reported this again to the police. Chinese detective Wang Chengying disguised himself as a rickshaw puller, and detective Wu Changkai disguised himself as a chauffeur. Detective Zhang Yaoji, posing as Zhang's representative, secretly went to the location. Together with French Concession detectives, they laid an ambush on all sides. Before long, three bandits were seen slowly approaching from Zilai Street opposite. Two bandits stood still at the Avenue Edward VII intersection, acting as lookouts, while one went forward to speak with Detective Zhang and accepted the package, at which point he was arrested. The lookouts were also apprehended. All three were taken to the French Concession police station and then transferred to the Xin Zha police station. After interrogation, the bandit who approached was identified as Que Wenda from Suzhou, also known as Li Jianhong. The two lookouts were named Wang Shuping (also known as Yue Ying, from Haimen) and Wu Zhanlin (also known as Jin Rongsheng, from Nanjing). They confessed to conspiring to extort money, and their statements were recorded. They were ordered to be detained. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The police lawyer Qian Xunjiu presented the case and submitted the statements, requesting a postponement for further investigation. The court approved the detention. Zhang Shangyi also sent a representative to the court to describe everything. When questioned, the defendant Que Wenda confessed that he knew Wang and Wu. He stated that the whole thing was his own idea. He obtained Zhang Shangyi's address from the telephone book and, using the alias Li Jianhong, wrote letters requesting a loan of five thousand dollars. All previous letters were written by him alone. It was not until the 28th of last month that he told Wang and Wu about the matter at the Changle Tea House and discussed plans. However, by that time, he had already sent five letters and made three phone calls, he claimed. Wang Shuping and Wu Zhanlin both vehemently denied knowing Que, saying they were strangers to him and had nothing to do with the matter. They claimed his words were all lies and that they knew nothing about the threatening letters. They were arrested while passing by the area yesterday. Judge Wu Tingqi reviewed the confessions and ordered all three defendants to be detained.

Japanese National Illegally Manufactures Morphine

Chinese Accomplices Sentenced and Fined

Chief of the Chinese Detective Division of the Public Concession Police, Wang Changgen, and Cao Bingkun, learned on the 23rd of last month that someone was manufacturing morphine equipment at No. 18 West Jiaxing Road to sell to other places for profit. They joined forces with narcotics officers Song Bingzheng, and Chief Inspector Pan Gensi and went to the address in secret. There they arrested the principal offender, a Japanese national named Nakamura, and turned him over to the Japanese consulate for interrogation. Nine Chinese accomplices, Fang Yinbao, Lin Huiqing, Su Ahui, Diao Jinsheng, and cook Wang Kaiyan, along with a large quantity of morphine drugs worth over thirty-five thousand dollars, as well as various machines, tools, wooden boxes, and other items, were taken to the Hongkou police station and transferred to the First Special District Court. After interrogation, the case was ready for sentencing. Yesterday morning, Judge Qiao Wanxuan presided over a hearing and sentenced Fang Yinbao, Lin Huiqing, Zhou Yongyuan, Yang Xiuwen, Guo Yuming, and Chen Ruikang to one year and six months in prison and fined them three thousand dollars each for jointly manufacturing opium substitutes. Su Ahui and Diao Jinsheng were sentenced to one year in prison and fined two thousand dollars each for jointly assisting in the manufacture of opium substitutes. If they chose imprisonment instead of paying the fines, the fines would be converted to imprisonment based on the total fine amount divided by the number of days in a year. The number of days the defendants were detained before the verdict was confirmed would be counted as two days of imprisonment for one day of the sentence. The morphine equipment and other items were confiscated according to the list. Wang Kaiyan was found not guilty. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated that Wang should be returned to police custody during the appeal period. The court approved.

Recent Work of the YMCA

Academic Lectures: To instill knowledge, the Shanghai YMCA initiated a series of academic lectures held every Sunday afternoon at 2:30 PM. Four sessions have already been successfully held, with renowned contemporary figures as speakers, attracting a large audience. The fifth series of lectures was originally scheduled for the spring, but was postponed due to the outbreak of the Shanghai War. Now that social order has been restored, the YMCA has decided to continue the program, starting on June 12th and continuing until August 7th, with the overall theme of "Domestic Peace," divided into nine lectures. The speakers are expected to be Mr. Liu Zhanen, Lin Kanghou, Zhu Maocheng, Wang Xiaolai, He Shangping, Yu Rizhang, Chen Liting, Hu Shuhua, and Liu Wang Liming. It is now summer vacation, and students have a lot of free time, so the number of attendees is expected to be even greater than before. The first lecture of the fifth series is scheduled for this Sunday afternoon at 2:30 PM, with the topic "Non-War and Construction," presented by Dr. Liu Zhanen, President of Shanghai University. The topic is of pressing importance today, and all Chinese people are eagerly hoping for progress. All those wishing to attend are welcome to the new YMCA location at Baixianqiao.

Radio Broadcast Lectures: The Shanghai YMCA has recently observed the increasing number of people with radio equipment. Merely broadcasting songs only provides entertainment and does not benefit the mind and body. Therefore, the YMCA has decided to utilize radio broadcasting to transmit lectures every Sunday morning from 10:00 AM to 11:00 AM on the Huadong Company broadcasting station. Various topics related to politics, current events, economics, and society will be presented by invited experts. Last week, Mr. Chen Liting reported on "The Visit of the League of Nations Investigation Team to the Three Northeastern Provinces." This Sunday, Mr. Yu Hongjun, Secretary-General of the Shanghai Municipal Government, has been specially invited to report on "The Shanghai Incident." All those with radio receivers are urged not to miss this excellent opportunity.

Dongdong Hosiery Factory Clearance Sale Ending Soon

The main branch of the Dongdong Hosiery Factory on Nanjing Road and the Nan branch inside Xiaodongmen have been holding a grand clearance sale and giving away gifts for the past fourteen days since June 5th. The factory is usually not inclined to offer discounts, so this sale has been particularly popular. The attached clearance department has been especially busy, with seasonal summer items such as ramie shirts and trousers, silk and cotton socks, and Parisian cosmetics selling in large quantities every day. The courteous service of the factory staff has also greatly satisfied customers. The clearance sale and gift promotion will only last for seven more days. After that, there will be no extension.

Excellent Contributions from the Manufacturing Sector

Since the January 28th Incident, all compatriots have been filled with righteous indignation, sharing a common hatred and vowing never to forget this humiliation. In light of this, the Peide Necktie Factory has invented the "January 28th" Western-style cufflinks, which are finely crafted, smooth, elegant, exquisite, and durable, as well as being of high quality and low price. They truly lead the way in the domestic goods manufacturing sector. The main purpose is to promote domestic goods, resist foreign imports, and allow the Chinese people to permanently commemorate the January 28th tragedy. Western-style clothing people are extremely satisfied with their purchase, so they are selling very well in the market.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that a land depression is coming from the Yangtze River basin and will reach the coast tonight. A typhoon in the Pacific Ocean is moving north and has reached northeast of Taiwan, causing severe weather conditions throughout the East China Sea and around the Ryukyu Islands. Gusts of wind are expected in this area tonight. The middle reaches of the Yangtze River have cloudy and rainy weather, but it is gradually clearing, and tomorrow morning it may become cloudy with light and erratic winds. Severe weather conditions will continue at the mouth of the Yangtze River. The Shandong coast is cloudy with occasional winds from the south. The Taiwan Strait is cloudy with gentle southwest winds. As of noon, the center of the typhoon was located within 60 miles of the intersection of 26 degrees north latitude and 125 degrees east longitude. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this area was 80.1 degrees and the lowest was 67.3 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 80.6 degrees and the lowest was 66.7 degrees.

Comment

Talking About Family Matters

— Fo

The big family system has long been recognized as unsuitable for modern trends. The small family system should emerge in response.

"Five generations under one roof" and "eight generations not separated" sound good in name, but a closer examination of their content reveals discord between sisters-in-law, opposition between mothers-in-law, and even brothers may not be able to live in harmony. One criticizes the other for spending too much, while the other boasts about their living conditions. Internal conflicts are bound to be fierce, but bound by the old ethics and held hostage by the head of the family, they have no choice but to endure.

Now, the names "five generations under one roof" and "eight generations not separated" are no longer sufficient to rally people and cannot be considered good stories. Even the authority of the head of the family cannot govern the entire family. "Fratricide" and "sibling rivalry" occur, with younger brothers disowning older brothers and mothers-in-law bullying daughters-in-law. Within the family, complaints are often heard. "When the fence is broken, wild dogs come in." Bandits and thugs take advantage of the situation. A good family is reduced to a mess.

Judging from the current situation, organizing small families is more appropriate. Establishing the principle of "everyone sweeps the snow in front of their own door and doesn't care about the frost on the roof of others," each household sets up its own business, produces its own goods, and strives on its own. Perhaps the family can achieve modest prosperity one day.

If we continue to struggle to maintain the empty façade of "five generations under one roof" and "eight generations not separated," I fear that the family will be completely destroyed.

Literature and Art

Crying Willow Chen

— Zhu Zun

A strong wind blows through willow branches, only making a soft sound.

Self-proclaimed softness overcomes strength, this principle is indeed unparalleled.

Pines and cypresses hear it and weep, I am born strong and independent.

I would rather be broken into a thousand pieces than be swayed by the wind.

Hearing the Cuckoo

Transformed into millions of souls, how many cuckoos are newly added?

Crying non-stop day and night, the tears of travelers fall drop by drop.

Compared to last year's cries, there seem to be countless more grievances.

Don't call to return home, guard the national gate in life and death.

National Mourning

In memory of the fallen soldiers in the Shanghai Anti-Japanese War

In life, I wish to be soil, to bury the souls of national martyrs.

In poetry, I wish to be a lament, to mourn the grievances of national martyrs.

Brave soldiers died for the country, their spirits will live on forever.

The Chinese are not a weak race, thanks to you for making it clear.

Bitter was the thirty-day battle, repeatedly pursuing the powerful enemy.

Sad were the traitors who appeased the enemy, providing no assistance for thirty days.

Your achievements were almost successful, the people of the country share the grief.

Offering distant condolences in the wind, you will forever be the god of national warfare.

Science

How to Install a Lightning Rod

— Yun Li

Dear readers! In the previous article "What is Lightning?", I told you that when two kinds of electricity with different yin and yang properties come into contact in the air, they not only produce an explosive sound but also can harm people, animals, and buildings on the ground. From this perspective, this kind of electricity is extremely dangerous. But, what methods can we use to avoid it?

In 1752 AD, 178 years ago, the famous American scientist Benjamin Franklin invented the lightning rod after experimenting with electricity in the air using a kite.

, used to protect houses and the people and animals inside, so now most tall buildings have this kind of lightning rod installed.

A lightning rod is a metal rod (Note). Its installation method is to place this metal rod at the highest point of the roof. The upper end of the metal is sharp, and the lower end is connected to a metal wire; the lower end of the metal wire is connected to several metal plates. Then bury these metal plates in the dampest place underground. Because the ground is damp, it is easier to conduct electricity.

With a lightning rod installed on the roof, how can we avoid the danger of electricity? However, we must understand; all substances contain electricity, and this metal rod naturally contains electricity as well. The reason why we don't usually feel electricity is because the amounts of yin and yang electricity are balanced, that is, they are harmonized, which is what electrical scientists call "neutralization."

If there is a thunderstorm, the electricity in the clouds is harmful because the amounts of yin and yang electricity are not balanced. The excess electricity will attract the opposite type of lightning that is lacking. That is, an excess of positive electricity will attract negative electricity, and an excess of negative electricity will attract positive electricity, so the danger of lightning arises.

To avoid this danger of electricity, we only need to use a lightning rod to eliminate the excess positive lightning or excess negative electricity. Because the upper end of the needle is sharp, it is easy to discharge electricity. When a cloud carrying an excess of negative electricity comes near the lightning rod, the positive electricity contained in the needle is released from the tip of the needle due to induction, neutralizing the electricity in the clouds and causing it to disappear; the remaining part of the negative electricity in the needle is transmitted to the ground through the metal wire. If the cloud carries positive electricity, the lightning rod will release negative electricity to neutralize it; the remaining part of the positive electricity is transmitted to the ground through the metal wire. In short, whether it brings positive lightning or negative electricity, it always releases electricity of the opposite polarity to neutralize it, so it can avoid the danger of lightning.

Why does the bottom of the lightning rod need to be connected to some metal sheets buried in the dampest underground? This is because during a heavy thunderstorm, when clouds carrying negative electricity come near the needle, the positive electricity on the needle is released from the tip of the needle, leaving an excess of negative electricity; if clouds carrying positive electricity come near the needle, the negative electricity on the needle is released from the tip of the needle, leaving an excess of positive electricity. The excess negative electricity

or positive electricity left in this way must be sent to the ground through a metal wire in order to completely avoid danger. Therefore, those metal sheets must be buried in the dampest underground. If they are buried in dry underground, the lightning rod will lose its effectiveness. Because dry land is not a good conductor and does not easily transmit lightning.

In addition to the above-mentioned installation method, there is another way to install a lightning rod. That is to make the metal wire into a mesh shape and cover it on the upper part of the house to avoid the disaster of lightning, but in any case, a metal wire must be used to connect several metal plates to the ground.

(Note) Substances such as gold, silver, copper, iron, and tin are all called metals. Red copper is best for making lightning rods.

A Corner of Society

(5) A Tour of ×× Company

— Yi Ping

The long hand points directly at eleven o'clock, five minutes short of leaving the office, Xiao Wenying's heart is beating rapidly? He remembers Yuan Jinzhi's Introduction to Gambling, which is much more fun than the dead salary of sitting in the office, he tidies up the things on his desk, preparing for the clanging of the clock.

The two walked side by side towards ×× Company, Yuan Jinzhi talked about the stories of women as if nothing had happened, although Xiao Wenying was eager to understand the situation of ×× Company, but there was no room for him to interject, he only heard him suddenly say softly "We're here" It is the ××× intersection that is often walked, several special figures wearing black long gowns always sit idly at the door.

He lowered his head and followed Jinzhi through a long corridor, and he heard noisy sounds coming from every crowd, he really wanted to squeeze in to see what it was like, who knew that Jinzhi had stepped onto the stairs facing the corridor, without any experience, he had no choice but to follow the experienced guide up another floor.

The upstairs and downstairs are completely different, like entering a women's country, many Shanghai women who do business with cosmetics stores every day, with their charming eyes, watching the balls in the plate roll into the number of their own pressed cakes, although like a champagne ticket, there is one number that occupies the final victory, but many disappointed expressions first chilled the heat of Xiao Wenying when he came in.

Yuan Jinzhi bought thirty yuan worth of numbers, as if he was managing bookkeeping in the company every day, engaging in a battle with fate on the Arabic numerals, Wenying held the banknotes in his pocket and was always hesitant and did not have the courage to take them out, thinking that Jinzhi, who had written the Introduction to Gambling, spent thirty yuan rolling into Guangdong Bank in the sound of the bell... (probably the gambling bosses who talk about gambling classics all know the allusion of Guangdong Bank) his forehead was like a customer who had entered the ice-drinking room, he walked out slowly as if he was going to the West Cannon Platform, and forgot that there was a Xiao Wenying behind him who was relying on him as an experienced guide.

Coming out of the company one after another, each with different emotions, disappearing into the shadows.

Ah Cun Jingli

A Youth and a Beggar

— Yin

On a street with few pedestrians, there were only one or two filthy and ragged beggars sitting under the eaves of people's houses, looking for lice the size of wheat grains on their bodies, and repeatedly putting them in their mouths, the way they looked, compared to modern men and women eating Western food together, was several times more interesting,

From afar came the sound of clattering leather shoes, gradually from far to near, the beggar immediately stopped catching lice, stood up, and greeted the young man wearing leather shoes,

"Good sir, may you be blessed and live a long life, do a good deed丨" he said very sincerely,

"·······" The young man continued to walk as if no one was there,

"Alas, sir, I haven't eaten for two days, do a good deed" he said with a mournful face, showing a very pitiful appearance,

"······" The young man walked away without looking back,

The sound of clattering leather shoes gradually went from near to far again, the poor beggar, waited until he could no longer see his shadow, before walking back to where he was originally sitting in disappointment to do his lice-catching work,

Tomorrow I saw the young man wearing leather shoes again, following behind a beautiful student-like girl in ×× Park, this is probably what Shanghai people call stalking,

"Miss, what is your name, what school do you go to, can we be friends?" he asked very sincerely,

"······" She continued to walk as if no one was there, "Alas Miss now that social interaction is open, men and women are equal, it doesn't matter if we become friends, why don't you pay attention to me, ······" he said very eagerly,

"······" She walked out of the park gate without looking back,

He stood at the door, watching her back, going far away, before taking a breath, and walking into the park in disappointment, still acting like a rickshaw man,

The Problem of Livelihood

A Sketch of Life

— Yun Zhi

"Madam, why don't you buy it, there are only twelve catties in total, consider it doing a good deed," said an old country woman in tattered clothes,

"You sell broad beans, I have copper coins and you have goods, why do you say such pitiful things?" A wealthy country lady asked suspiciously,

"No, madam, if you buy it, I still have to quickly pick up another load and sell it again丨"

"Why are you in such a hurry?"

"Because I need at least three dollars urgently tomorrow, and I don't have a single penny in hand yet,"

"What do you need three dollars for urgently?"

"Because I have hired six helpers at home to plant sweet potatoes tomorrow, I need at least three dollars, and I still owe the money for 20,000 sweet potato seedlings,"

"Don't you still have people at home?"

"Alas, don't even mention it, a son raised to eighteen years old, carried a load of salt to the town to sell, because his father was sick, who knew he would be taken away by the smugglers, not only was the salt confiscated, but he was also beaten, he couldn't stand seeing his son sick and dying, a wife who was married, was taken back to her maiden family from then on, now there are only two old bones left for us, a couple in their sixties, but they refuse to die, if we are alive, we have to eat," said the old woman, her eyes turning red,

"How much field do you need to plant now for the old couple to eat?" The lady asked pitifully, "When my son was alive, we rented sixteen acres of fields, now we have to return it to others to plant, and we only plant ten acres ourselves, after paying six dollars per acre for rent, it's really impossible to live this year," said the old woman, her eyes turning red again,

"Okay, then you sell all these broad beans to us, here, here's the money,"

"Good, truly Amitabha,"

"Oh, I've talked too much, I'm still in a hurry to go home," said the old woman, taking the money and leaving in a hurry, (Quotations)

A Karmic Bond

Miss Muxian Who Wants But Cannot Help It

Is it because there is freedom of marriage between men and women today, so I feel the pain of old-style marriage, or is it that old-style marriage has always been painful? This major problem, the painful problem, like a seventeen-year-old girl, I can't solve it after all,

My good classmate, lives near my neighborhood, Yimeng who was born in the same year as me, fortunately, is getting married at the end of this month, ever since she knew her wedding date ten days ago, she has been crying and weeping, and her face has been washed with tears all day long, her two eye bags are already like walnuts, she is not worried because she is young and suddenly leaves the embrace of her kind and loving parents and is sent to her husband's family where she is unfamiliar, nor is she used to being pampered at home, but she is given a poor husband, which is not the case at all,

Her only reason, is that her parents forced her to choose a spouse, so she is absolutely dissatisfied,

Her husband's family can be regarded as a deformed family, pieced together successfully, except for her father-in-law, her mother-in-law is a concubine, and her future husband is an adopted son, her father-in-law also has a secret little wife who is married outside, now living in the house, and already has children, and her mother-in-law also has a daughter born to her former husband, although she has married someone, because her son-in-law does not produce anything, she still relies on her father-in-law for a living,

When Yimeng was young, her father-in-law was still a peddler, he lived in a low house near a good family, because he was lucky in wealth, developed one day after another, and now he has a little family property, Yimeng's father, seeing that he had money, gave his daughter to him to be his daughter-in-law, at that time she was young and didn't understand anything, until in the recent three or four years, what day has she not been opposed to this marriage, she has raised objections to her parents several times, crying and weeping, and she has not been satisfied with this marriage, she has used all her methods, sometimes she pleads with her parents, sometimes she uses righteousness to touch her parents, but she is always disappointed, and she does not get results, the most recent time, she used her own life to scare them, not only did she not get her parents' love, but she was suppressed with violence,

This time her wedding date is so urgent, as far as I know, her mother-in-law is very seriously ill, and the doctor has given up, so they are eager to marry a daughter-in-law, in preparation for her to wear plain clothes and mourning after her death,

My dear Yimeng, I really want but cannot help it, how can I help you,

Civil Judgments: Gu Jingqing vs. Chen Shuqing for compensation - The respondent shall compensate the petitioner eight yuan, two jiao, and one fen in litigation costs; the petitioner's remaining claims are rejected. ▲ Li Yunquan vs. Liu Yixiang et al. for loan - The defendant Peng Shuiji shall repay the plaintiff a loan of seven hundred yuan and interest at a rate of 1.2% per month from January 12, 1932, until the date of execution; the plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected. Peng Shuiji is responsible for the litigation costs. ▲ Jiang Zhicheng et al. vs. Cao Wu Shi et al. for compensation - The plaintiffs' claims are rejected; the litigation costs are to be borne equally by the plaintiffs. ▲ Xu Mujin vs. Fang Jiahe for public expense retrial - The retrial is rejected; the retrial costs are borne by the retrial plaintiff. ▲ Shen Zhixian vs. Song Shaolan for compensation for damages - The plaintiff's claims are rejected; the litigation costs are borne by the plaintiff. ▲ Yin Shusheng vs. Chao Kunbao for rent appeal - The appeal is rejected; the first instance litigation costs are borne by the appellant. ▲ Su Yunqing vs. Yang Ziwen for rent - The defendant shall repay the plaintiff ninety-two yuan in rent and shall vacate the premises and return them to the plaintiff; the litigation costs, except for one-fifth of the withdrawn portion borne by the plaintiff, shall be borne four-fifths by the defendant. ▲ Zheng Guangrong vs. Li Hanchen for rent - The defendant shall repay the plaintiff forty-four yuan in rent, plus eighty-eight jiao in small yuan, and shall immediately vacate the premises; the litigation costs are borne by the defendant. The first item of this judgment shall be subject to provisional execution. ▲ Zhang Dexian vs. Zhao Shisheng for mortgage loan - The plaintiff's claims are rejected; the litigation costs are borne by the plaintiff. ▲ Zhou Jianhua vs. Song Liangcai for alimony - The defendant shall pay the plaintiff five hundred yuan in alimony; the plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected; the litigation costs are borne equally by both parties. ▲ Zhu Rundong vs. Zhu Yizhi for contract - It is confirmed that the rights under the agreement entered into by the plaintiff and defendant on February 9, 1928, shall exist; the litigation costs are borne by the defendant.

Civil Judgments: Qu Ronggen et al. vs. Qu Yougen for division of property and payment of marriage expenses - Qu Xiaoyun's estate, located in Shangyi, 125 Bao, 9 Tu, consisting of three pieces of land totaling one mu, six fen, one li, five hao, and three hu, together with a building and outbuildings, shall be divided in half by the defendant to the plaintiff. The 1,200 yuan borrowed by Qu Xiaoyun to Xu Xingsheng shall be assigned to Qu Jinmei; furthermore, the 600 yuan borrowed by Qu Xiaoyun to Xiao Yangzhou, 200 yuan to Wang Mao Nv, and 300 yuan to Shi Amao shall be assigned to Qu Yousheng. The litigation costs are borne by the defendant. ▲ Yitai Construction Company Chen Rubo vs. Wang Yanwei for compensation for damages and request for restoration of the original state - The petition is rejected; the petition costs are borne by the petitioner. ▲ Xinruihe Foreign Firm vs. Dahonglou Restaurant for rent arrears - The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 880 taels of silver; the litigation costs are borne by the defendant. ▲ Zhenda Needlework Factory Zhang Xinkang vs. Fucheng Hao Zhuang Yisan for payment of goods - The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 380 taels and eight qian in goods; the litigation costs are borne by the defendant. ▲ Ruiyu Rice Shop vs. Li Dewen for loan - The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 300 yuan and pay interest at a rate of 2% per annum from May 16, 1930, until the date of execution; the litigation costs are borne by the defendant. ▲ Qian Wenqi vs. Cao Mao Shi et al. for rent and termination of lease - The defendant Cao Mao Shi shall pay the plaintiff 276 yuan in rent; the defendant Chen Dixing shall pay the plaintiff 112.5 yuan in rent. If execution is ineffective, the defendant Peng Huating shall pay on their behalf. The plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected; the plaintiff bears one-third of the litigation costs, and the remaining costs are borne proportionally by the defendants Cao Mao Shi and Chen Dixing. ▲ Xie Shengzu vs. Lin Muzhen for rent arrears and eviction - The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 990 taels of silver in rent and return the leased premises to the plaintiff; the litigation costs are borne by the defendant. Regarding the return of the leased premises in the first item of this judgment, provisional execution shall be granted. ▲ Shanghai Yuhua Refined Salt Company vs. Yongxiang Xiaoji Company Sun Jiamao for guarantee of debt - The defendant shall compensate the plaintiff for 1,290 silver yuan that Wang Zhixian should have compensated, and if Wang Zhixian cannot pay, the defendant shall pay on his behalf; the litigation costs are borne by the defendant. ▲ Xinkang Company vs. Ying Zhongxiu for rent and return of property - The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 240 yuan in rent and return the premises at No. 2, Donglin Lane, Jiaxiyi Road to the plaintiff; the litigation costs are borne by the defendant. Regarding the return of the leased premises in this judgment, provisional execution may be granted. ▲ China Business Company vs. Aiterson et al. for rent arrears - The defendant Aiterson shall repay the plaintiff 80 taels of silver in rent; Fan Lou Yunqin shall repay the plaintiff 255 taels of silver in rent; Li Datong shall repay the plaintiff 196 taels of silver in rent; Wang Yuanbo shall repay the plaintiff 94 taels of silver in rent; the litigation costs, except for the withdrawn portion borne by the plaintiff, are borne proportionally by the defendants. ▲ Wu Changgeng vs. Zhang Jiantang for payment of goods - The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 1,031 yuan, six jiao, and eight fen; the litigation costs are borne by the defendant. ▲ Zhu Riman Bide vs. Rabobote for debt - The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 401 yuan and six jiao in Japanese currency; the litigation costs are borne by the defendant. Provisional execution may be granted for this judgment. ▲ Changli Company Chen Shanzhang vs. Yuan Chengji et al. for contract termination and rent recovery - The defendants shall immediately terminate the contract and vacate the premises, and each shall repay the plaintiff a total of 13,449 yuan and six jiao according to the amount of rent owed; the litigation costs are borne proportionally by the defendants. The plaintiff's request for provisional execution is rejected. ▲ Nama Ka vs. Mrs. Tang for repair costs - The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 110 taels and five qian in silver; the litigation costs are borne by the defendant. ▲ Xu Shunbao vs. Feng Xiangmao for debt - The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 184 yuan and nine jiao and five fen; the litigation costs are borne by the defendant. ▲ Bi Haogeng vs. Du Xingsheng for rent arrears - The defendant shall pay the plaintiff 28 yuan in rent; the litigation costs are borne by the defendant.
